Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Introducing Al-Tawdih wa Al-Talwih and Their Urdu Commentary
Title page introducing the book

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the foundational texts of Hanafi usul al-fiqh (Al-Tawdih wa Al-Talwih) and explain the role of commentaries in the Hanafi scholarly tradition.

Core Idea
Al-Tawdih wa Al-Talwih are the backbone of Hanafi usul al-fiqh; mastering them begins with understanding their place in the curriculum.

This lesson introduces you to the text you will be studying: an Urdu commentary on Al-Tawdih wa Al-Talwih. These two works—Al-Tawdih by Sadr al-Shariah and Al-Talwih by al-Taftazani—are among the most difficult and most important texts in Hanafi usul al-fiqh. Understanding what this commentary aims to do will help you approach the study with the right expectations.

Guided Path
1
Identify the Work
The title page states this is a commentary on Al-Tawdih wa Al-Talwih. These are two distinct but related works. Al-Tawdih is the base text, and Al-Talwih is a super-commentary.
Al-Tawdih was written by Sadr al-Shariah (d. 747 AH) and Al-Talwih by Sa'd al-Din al-Taftazani (d. 792 AH).
2
Understand the Authors and Their Relationship
Sadr al-Shariah was a Hanafi jurist and usuli; al-Taftazani was a master of logic, kalam, and rhetoric. Al-Talwih is a commentary on Al-Tawdih, meaning it explains and occasionally critiques the earlier work.
This layered authorship is typical of the Hanafi tradition: each generation builds on the previous.
3
Recognize the Curriculum Context
The commentary is prepared for the syllabus of Wifaq al-Madaris, the major board of Islamic seminaries in Pakistan. This indicates its importance in advanced Hanafi studies.
Wifaq al-Madaris prescribes a set curriculum; this book is a key text for usul al-fiqh.
4
Note the Commentator's Credentials
Maulana Muhammad Luqman is described as 'teacher of scholars' and an expert in grammar and logic. This signals the depth required to explain these texts.
The commentator's background in grammar (nahw) is essential for parsing the terse Arabic of the original.
5
Preview Special Features
The title page lists features like translation, parsing, grammatical analysis, and metaphors. This shows the commentary aims to make the difficult text accessible to Urdu-speaking students.
These features are pedagogical tools to bridge the gap between the classical Arabic text and the student.

Commentary
This passage is the title page and introductory material of the book. It identifies the work as an Urdu commentary (sharh) on Al-Tawdih wa Al-Talwih, which are foundational texts in Hanafi usul al-fiqh. Al-Tawdih was written by Sadr al-Shariah, and Al-Talwih is a super-commentary by Sa'd al-Din al-Taftazani. This commentary aims to make the difficult text accessible to students studying under the Wifaq al-Madaris syllabus. The author, Maulana Muhammad Luqman, is described as a teacher of scholars and an expert in grammar and logic. The publisher is Maktab al-Husaynayn. The page contains some garbled OCR text but the overall intent is clear: this is the cover page introducing the book.

Key Terms
التوضيح (Al-Tawdih): A foundational Hanafi usul al-fiqh text by Sadr al-Shariah (d. 747 AH).
التلويح (Al-Talwih): A super-commentary on Al-Tawdih by Sa'd al-Din al-Taftazani (d. 792 AH).
شرح (Sharh): A commentary that explains a base text, often line by line.

Al-Tawdih wa Al-Talwih are foundational texts in Hanafi usul al-fiqh, and this Urdu commentary aims to make them accessible.

Navigating the Fihrist: Understanding the Scope of Al-Tarweeh
Table of contents listing topics and page numbers

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to locate and describe the major topics covered in Al-Tarweeh li-Hall al-Tawdeeh wa al-Talweeh and relate them to the broader discipline of Hanafi usul al-fiqh.

Core Idea
A table of contents is a roadmap to the science – it reveals the structure, priorities, and breadth of Hanafi usul al-fiqh.

This lesson examines the table of contents (فہرست مضامین) of a major Hanafi usul al-fiqh commentary, Al-Tarweeh. While a TOC may seem trivial, it provides invaluable insight into the book's organization and the author's approach. By studying this fihrist, you will gain a bird's-eye view of the key debates, figures, and methodologies that define Hanafi legal theory.

Guided Path
1
Identify the book and its genre
Recognise that this is a commentary (sharh) on usul al-fiqh, specifically glossing al-Tawdeeh wa al-Talweeh. The TOC shows it is a comprehensive work.
The full title indicates the type of work (sharh) and the base texts.
2
Scan the major divisions
Notice the sequence: endorsements, introduction, definition, necessity, biographies, and then detailed topics like linguistic investigations and metaphors.
The TOC orders topics thematically, not necessarily by chapter number.
3
Highlight key topics
Identify recurring themes: definitions (entry 3), biographical entries (9-13), linguistic analysis (18, 23, 27-28), and specific debates (14-15).
This reveals the author's emphasis on both foundational concepts and detailed linguistic points.
4
Map biographies to historical context
Understand the chain of scholars: Allama Bazdawi, Imam Razi, Ibn Hajib, Taftazani – key figures in Hanafi usul. This situates the commentary within a tradition.
The TOC shows that the book engages with earlier authorities.
5
Reflect on the structure's purpose
Consider why the author included certain topics: the 'wisdom of legislating analogy' (25) and 'cause for specifying the art' (30) indicate a focus on the rationale behind usul rules.
This structure helps the student understand not just the 'what' but the 'why' of Hanafi usul.

Commentary
This passage is a table of contents (فہرست مضامین) for the book 'Al-Tarweeh li-Hall al-Tawdeeh wa al-Talweeh', a commentary on the Hanafi usul al-fiqh work. It lists chapter headings and topics with corresponding page numbers, providing an overview of the book's structure. The first few entries cover general topics such as the definition of usul al-fiqh, its necessity, and biographies of key scholars like Allama Bazdawi, Imam Razi, and Ibn Hajib. Later entries delve into detailed linguistic and conceptual analyses, including discussions on metaphor (استعارہ), the wisdom of analogy (قیاس), and the author's purpose. Some page numbers appear corrupted in the scan, but the content outline remains clear.

Key Terms
فہرست مضامین (fihrist-e-mawāḍī'): A list of topics or table of contents indicating the structure of the book.
اصول فقہ (uṣūl al-fiqh): The principles of Islamic jurisprudence – the methodology used to derive rulings from the primary sources.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Navigating the Table of Contents of al-Tarwih
Index listing chapter headings and page numbers.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to interpret the table of contents of a classical usul al-fiqh text and identify the types of linguistic analysis it covers.

Core Idea
A table of contents reveals the structural and methodological blueprint of a usul work.

This passage is the table of contents of the book 'Al-Tarwih li-Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih', a commentary on al-Tawdih and al-Talwih. It lists the main topics and their page numbers, giving us an overview of the author's analytical approach. By studying this index, we can understand the scope of the work and the categories of research it employs.

Guided Path
1
Scan the topics listed
Quickly review all entries to get a sense of the range of subjects covered.
Notice repeated terms like 'لغوی تحقیق' and 'استعارات'.
2
Identify the categories of research
Note the distinct types: lexical research (لغوی تحقیق), syntactic research (ترکیبی تحقیق), intentional research (مرادی تحقیق), and metaphors (استعارات).
These categories form the backbone of the author's methodology.
3
Recognize the book's structure
See that it starts with the sermon (خطبہ) and progresses through various discussions, indicating a commentary structure.
The table of contents is a roadmap for the entire text.

Commentary
This passage is the table of contents (fihrist) of the book 'Al-Tarwih li-Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. It lists the main topics and their corresponding page numbers, giving an overview of the book's structure. The topics include lexical, syntactic, and intentional investigations, discussions on metaphors (isti‘arat), research on specific phrases, reasons for compiling the book, and an index of the degrees of expertise in usul al-fiqh. The table of contents helps the reader navigate the work and understand its scope.

Key Terms
استعارات (isti‘arat): Metaphorical usages in Arabic, discussed linguistically.
لغوی تحقیق (lughawi tahqiq): Lexical research or linguistic analysis of terms.
ترکیبی تحقیق (tarkibi tahqiq): Syntactic analysis of word structures.
مرادی تحقیق (muradi tahqiq): Intentional analysis, focusing on the speaker's intent.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Key Takeaway
The table of contents of al-Tarwih reveals the author's emphasis on lexical, syntactic, and intentional analyses as foundational to usul al-fiqh.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner

Navigating Al-Tarweeh: Understanding Its Table of Contents
Table of contents listing topics and page numbers.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to locate specific topics within Al-Tarweeh li-hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih using its table of contents and explain the purpose of a maddamin in a classical Hanafi usul text.

Core Idea
A table of contents is the map of a classical text; it reveals the author's structure and priorities.

This passage is the table of contents (maddamin) from Al-Tarweeh, a Hanafi usul al-fiqh commentary. It lists topics and their page numbers, allowing you to quickly find discussions on key concepts like the definition of usul, the three pillars, and Imam Abu Hanifa's definition of fiqh. Understanding how to use this tool is essential for navigating the dense material in classical texts.

Guided Path
1
Identify the text type
Look at the layout: it is a list of topics with page numbers. This is a table of contents (maddamin), not a continuous exposition.
The Arabic heading 'مضامین' confirms this.
2
Locate major section headings
Scan for key terms like 'أصول الفقه', 'اركان', 'تعريف'. These indicate the main subjects covered in the book.
Major sections often have multiple subheadings.
3
Cross-reference page numbers
Notice the numbers after each topic. Use these to find the exact page in the text where the discussion begins.
Page numbers are sequential and may span multiple pages.
4
Note the sequence of topics
Observe the order of topics. This reflects the author's logical progression, from foundational definitions to detailed discussions.
The sequence helps you understand the structure of the commentary.
5
Recognize the structure of the commentary
The TOC shows that the author follows a pattern: definition, pillars, sub-discussions, and applications. This mirrors the typical Hanafi usul textbook structure.
Knowing this pattern aids in predicting content.

وجه حصر ارکان ثلاثه

Commentary
This is a table of contents (maddamin) from 'Altarweeh li-hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih', a Hanafi usul commentary. It lists topics across pages 11-12. Key headings include definitions of usul, discussions on the three pillars of fiqh, the meaning of 'asl', differences between real and relational essences, and definitions of fiqh by Imam Abu Hanifa. Also shows page references for sections on types of rulings, makruh tahrimi, etc. No legal analysis here—just a guide to the text's structure.

Key Terms
أصول الفقه (usul al-fiqh): The principles of jurisprudence, the foundational discipline for deriving fiqh rulings.

Introduction and Front Matter
intermediate
6 min
Navigating Altarweeh: Introduction to Hanafi Usul Topics
Table of contents listing topics and page numbers for Altarweeh

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the major topics covered in Altarweeh and explain how the taqsimat arba'ah structure organizes Hanafi usul al-fiqh discussions.

Core Idea
The four divisions of lafz (taqsimat arba'ah) are the backbone of Hanafi usul al-fiqh.

This lesson introduces the table of contents of Altarweeh, a key commentary on Al-Tawdih and Al-Talwih. By understanding the structure of topics, you will see how Hanafi usul al-fiqh is organized around the four divisions of lafz and related debates. Use this as a roadmap for your study.

Guided Path
1
Identify the book and its purpose
Altarweeh is a commentary (sharh) and gloss (hāshiya) on two foundational usul works: Al-Tawdih by Sadr al-Shariah and Al-Talwih by Taftazani. The table of contents reveals the sequence of topics discussed.
2
Scan the major thematic clusters
Look for recurring terms like 'taqsimat arba'ah' (four divisions), 'Fakhr al-Islam', 'Imam Abu Hanifa', and 'amr shakhsi' (personal command). These indicate the core discussions.
The four divisions are: mutlaq/muqayyad, amm/khass, nass/zahir, etc.
3
Note the page ranges for key debates
For example, pages 398-412 discuss the definition of 'amr' and the meaning of 'bahth'. Pages 413-439 focus on the four divisions and objections.
Use the page numbers to quickly locate specific arguments.
4
Recognize the centrality of the Quranic discussion
Many entries revolve around whether the Quran is only meaning (ma'na) or includes lafz. This is a distinctive Hanafi position attributed to Imam Abu Hanifa.
Compare with Shafi'i usul which emphasizes both.
5
Connect to your own study plan
Use this TOC as a checklist. As you progress through the text, mark off each topic you have mastered.
Focus on the taqsimat arba'ah as they appear frequently.

Source pages p. 23

Commentary
This window presents the table of contents (فہرست مضامین) of the book 'Altarweehurdu sharh Al-Tawdih wa Al-Talwih', which is a commentary and gloss on the usul al-fiqh works Al-Tawdih by Sadr al-Shariah and Al-Talwih by Taftazani. The contents list spans from page 398 to 502, summarizing the key topics discussed in the text. Major themes include: the definition of a personal command (امر شخصی), analysis of Ibn al-Hajib's definition, the arrangement of discussions on the Qur'an, the four divisions of lafz (تقسیمات اربعہ) based on its relation to meaning, discussions on whether the Qur'an is only meaning or lafz, the views of Imam Abu Hanifa and Fakhr al-Islam, and detailed treatment of each division. The table allows the reader to quickly locate specific discussions within the commentary.

Key Terms
مضامین (mazamin): contents or topics listed in the table of contents
تقسیمات اربعہ (taqsimat arba'ah): the four divisions of lafz (word) according to its relation to meaning: mutlaq/muqayyad, amm/khass, etc.
امر شخصی (amr shakhsi): personal command; a command addressed to a specific individual

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
Which of the following topics is explicitly listed in the table of contents?
A) The conditions of qiyas
B) Whether nazm and lafz are synonymous
C) The definition of ijma'
D) The number of Quranic verses

Key Takeaway
Use the table of contents to map the major usul topics and see how the four divisions of lafz tie the entire discourse together.

Introduction and Front Matter

Navigating the Index: Key Topics in Hanafi Usul al-Fiqh
Index of topics in the commentary on Al-Tawdih wa Al-Talwih

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the major usul al-fiqh topics listed in the table of contents of 'Al-Tarwih li-Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' and describe how they relate to the Hanafi legal tradition.

Core Idea
A table of contents is a roadmap: knowing the structure helps you navigate the detailed discussions of amm, khass, naskh, and other Hanafi principles.

This lesson introduces you to the table of contents of a major Hanafi usul commentary. While it may seem like a simple list, understanding the layout of topics like al-amm al-makhsus, the difference between takhsis and naskh, and the various expressions of umum will help you follow the logical progression of the book. This index is your guide to the rich discussions that follow.

Guided Path
1
Survey the overall structure
Notice the numbering from 503 to 546, indicating a sequence of discussions. This is not random but follows a logical order.
The numbers are likely page references in the original text.
2
Identify major thematic groups
Group topics: amm khass (504-509), naskh vs takhsis (508-514, 517-518), expressions of umum (519-546). This reveals the author's flow.
3
Recognize key terms
Note terms like 'amm, khass, naskh, takhsis, jam', nakirah, etc. These are core concepts in Hanafi usul.
Use a glossary to familiarize yourself.
4
Observe the use of examples
Topics 512-518 provide fiqhi examples of naskh and takhsis, showing how abstract principles apply to real cases.
The examples involve sale of slaves, a standard Hanafi illustration.
5
Prepare for deeper study
This index shows that the book thoroughly covers these concepts. As you read each section, refer back to this list to see how it fits into the bigger picture.

Source pages p. 28

Commentary
This passage is a table of contents (Mazameen) for the book 'Al-Tarwih li-Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih', covering pages 579 to 620 of the original text. It lists 44 topics (numbered 503 to 546) that form the headings of discussions in usul al-fiqh. The topics include: the nature of al-amm al-makhsus (general made specific) and whether it is qat'iy or zanni; the difference between takhsis and naskh; examples from fiqh (such as sale of two slaves) to illustrate naskh and takhsis; a chapter on expressions of umum (general terms) including jam' (plural), mufrad (singular), nakirah (indefinite) in various contexts (negation, condition, adjective). The list serves as a roadmap for the detailed discussions that follow in the main text. As a Hanafi usul work, this commentary (sharh) on Al-Tawdih wa Al-Talwih engages with the classical Hanafi positions on these topics.

Key Terms
عام (ʿāmm): A term that covers all individuals of its category; general.
خاص (khāṣṣ): A term specific to a particular individual or group.
نسخ (naskh): Abrogation: the replacement of a legal ruling by a later revealed text.
تخصیص (takhṣīṣ): Specification: restricting a general term to some of its individuals by evidence.
جمع (jamʿ): Plural form.
نکرہ (nakirah): Indefinite noun.

Key Terms from Source Passage

A well-structured table of contents is an essential tool for navigating a complex Hanafi usul text; it reveals the author's logical progression and key topics.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner

Dedication of the Work
Opening dedication of a Hanafi usul work

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain the significance of dedicating a scholarly work to the Prophet Muhammad and the author's teachers in the Hanafi tradition.

Core Idea
A scholarly work's dedication reflects its spiritual lineage and the author's debt to prophetic and scholarly guidance.

This lesson examines the opening dedication of Altarweeh li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih. The author first honors the Prophet Muhammad as the ultimate teacher, then acknowledges his own shaykhs. Such dedications are not mere formalities; they establish the work's chain of transmission and spiritual foundation.

Guided Path
1
Identify the two recipients
The dedication names the Prophet Muhammad and the author's teachers (shaykhs). Recognize that the Prophet is referred to as 'that teacher of humanity' and the teachers are mentioned as sources of spiritual blessing.
The Prophet's role as teacher is emphasized by the hadith 'innama bu'ithtu mu'alliman' (I was sent as a teacher).
2
Understand the hadith reference
The phrase 'innama bu'ithtu mu'alliman' is a well-known hadith highlighting the Prophet's mission as a teacher. This establishes the Prophet as the ultimate source of knowledge.
This hadith is often cited to emphasize the educational role of the Prophet.
3
Recognize the scholarly practice
Dedicating a work to one's teachers affirms the chain of transmission (sanad). In Islamic scholarship, knowledge is received through a line of teachers, and acknowledging them preserves the integrity of the transmission.
This practice is common in traditional Muslim scholarship, especially in the Hanafi school.
4
Reflect on the purpose
The dedication serves to seek blessings (barakah) through the Prophet and the teachers, and to express gratitude. It also sets a tone of humility and connection to the scholarly tradition.
Such dedications remind the reader that the author is part of a larger intellectual and spiritual community.

Source Text

التَّرُويْحُ لِحَلَّ التَّوْضِيحِ وَالتَّلْويج
انتساب
اس معلم انسانیت کے نام جس نے اِنَّمَا بعدتُ مُعَلما کا عملی نمونہ بن کر خلق خدا کو جہالت کے اندھیروں سے نکال کر شاہراہ
رشد و هدایت پر گامزن فرمایا
پھر ان مشائخ اور اساتذہ کرام کے نام جن کے فیوضات اور دعاؤں کی برکت سے بندہ کو تصنیفی میدان میں قدم رکھنے کی سعادت نصیب ہوئی
Altarweeh li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih
Dedication
In the name of that teacher of humanity who, by making the practical example of 'innama bu'ithtu mu'alliman', extracted God's creatures from the darkness of ignorance and set them on the highway of guidance and rectitude. Then, in the names of those noble shaykhs and teachers, through the blessings of whose effusions and prayers, this servant attained the honor of stepping into the field of authorship.
Source pages p. 31

Commentary
This page is a dedication. The author first dedicates his work to the Prophet Muhammad, described as the teacher of humanity who exemplified the hadith 'I was sent as a teacher.' Then he dedicates it to his own teachers and shaykhs, acknowledging that their spiritual grace and prayers enabled him to write this book. This is a common practice in Islamic scholarly works.

Key Terms
سانِد (sanad): Chain of transmission of knowledge, especially in hadith and fiqh, ensuring authenticity and continuity.
اجازہ (ijazah): License or permission to transmit knowledge, often granted by a teacher to a student.

Key Terms from Source Passage

B) To the Prophet Muhammad
C) To the Hanafi scholars
D) To the reader

Key Takeaway
The dedication affirms that true knowledge is received through a living chain of teachers, culminating in the Prophet.

Purpose and Endorsement of Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih
Dedication and endorsement for a commentary

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the purpose of the commentary 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' and identify the role of endorsements in Hanafi scholarly tradition.

Core Idea
This commentary simplifies a difficult usul text for students – a hallmark of Hanafi pedagogical care.

This passage opens 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' with a dedication to the Prophet and a note of appreciation from a later scholar. It explains why the author, Mawlana Muhammad Luqman, wrote this commentary: to make the challenging work 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' accessible. Understanding the front matter helps you appreciate the scholarly chain and the purpose of the book.

Guided Path
1
Identify the dedicatees
The author dedicates the work first to the Prophet Muhammad (peace be upon him) and then implicitly to his teachers. Note the opening: 'Muhammad wa fadli 'ala Rasulihi al-karim'.
Dedications often reflect the author's intellectual lineage.
2
Understand the book's purpose
The text states that 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' is a difficult but important textbook in hanafi usul al-fiqh. The author wrote this commentary to facilitate (tashil) and elaborate (tafsil) on it.
Tashil and tafsil are common goals in sharh literature.
3
Analyze the endorsement
The endorser, Javed Husayn, praises the work and prays for its benefit. He specifically mentions that he saw parts of it and found it beneficial (nafi') and excellent (ahsan).
Endorsements (taqriz) are traditional ways of validating a scholarly work.
4
Relate to the Hanafi tradition
This front matter places the commentary within the Hanafi usul tradition, showing continuity from the original text (by Sadr al-Shariah and Taftazani) to the present commentary.
Knowing the chain helps you trust the source.

In the name of Him, glorified and exalted. Muhammad and his family, upon his noble Messenger. To proceed: By the grace and favor of Allah the Exalted, He has granted our dear Mawlana Muhammad Luqman (may Allah preserve him) the taste for authorship along with the taste for teaching. The aforementioned Mawlana, with effort and sweat, authored this commentary to facilitate and elaborate upon it. Commentary
This passage is the front matter of the book 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. It consists of a dedication to the Prophet Muhammad (peace be upon him) and to the author's teachers, followed by a note of appreciation and endorsement by a later scholar, Mawlana Javed Husayn. The text explains that the author, Mawlana Muhammad Luqman, has written a commentary on the difficult text 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' (a classic Hanafi usul al-fiqh work) to make it easier for students. The endorser praises the work and prays for its acceptance and widespread benefit. This is introductory material and does not contain any technical fiqh rulings or usul principles. It sets the context for the scholarly commentary that follows.

Key Terms
توضیح تلویح (Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih): A classical text and super-commentary on Usul al-Fiqh in the Hanafi tradition, authored by Sadr al-Shariah and Taftazani.

Understanding Scholarly Endorsements (Taqriz) in Usul al-Fiqh Works
Endorsements (taqriz) for a usul commentary

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the purpose of taqriz and explain how endorsements attest to a book's scholarly value.

Core Idea
Scholarly endorsements (taqriz) certify a book's reliability and benefit — they are part of the Islamic academic tradition.

These pages contain endorsements from two respected scholars for the book 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih', a commentary on a classical usul text. While not a legal ruling, understanding taqriz helps you appreciate how the scholarly community validates and recommends works. This lesson explores the function of such endorsements.

Guided Path
1
Identify the content type
Recognize that these are endorsements (taqriz), not legal rulings. They serve as a certification of the book's quality.
Taqriz are customary in Islamic scholarly works.
2
Note the scholars and their credentials
The endorsers are teachers of Hadith and heads of institutions, lending authority to their praise.
Maulana Javed Hussain Shah and Maulana Muhammad Yaseen Sabir are well-known scholars.
3
Understand the aspects of praise
They highlight research quality, utility for students and teachers, and the author's hard work.
4
Connect to the usul context
The book is a sharh (commentary) on 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih', a key usul text. Endorsements signal that this commentary is reliable for studying usul.

Precious opinion: The possessor of both rational and transmitted sciences, the knower of wise symbols, the chief of teachers, our teacher Hazrat Maulana Muhammad Yaseen Sabir (may his blessings continue), teacher of Hadith, Jamia Umar ibn al-Khattab Multan. I found it highly research-oriented and quite interesting. In every era, scholars engage in academic works; by Allah's will this work is also happening now and will continue. Blessed are those great and selected individuals who are connected to this golden chain. I pray that Allah Almighty accepts this effort of the aforementioned Maulana and makes it most beneficial for students of knowledge and respected teachers. Amen, O Lord of the worlds, by the honor of the leader of the prophets and messengers (peace be upon him and his family and companions). Peace. The humble servant, Muhammad Yaseen Sabir, 18 Rabi al-Thani 1432 AH.

Commentary
These pages contain the endorsements (taqriz) of two respected scholars for the book 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih', which is a commentary (sharh) on the classical usul text 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. The first endorsement is by Hazrat Maulana Syed Javed Hussain Shah, who praises the author's dedication and the book's utility for students and teachers. The second endorsement is by Maulana Muhammad Yaseen Sabir, who commends the book's research quality and encourages its use. Such endorsements are customary in Islamic scholarly works to certify the book's reliability and benefit.

Key Terms

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
The Role of Taqriz in Hanafi Usul al-Fiqh Scholarship
Two scholarly endorsements for a Usul al-Fiqh commentary

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain the purpose and scholarly value of taqriz (endorsements) in the Hanafi tradition and identify how they authenticate a work.

Core Idea
Taqriz validates a text through recognized scholars, linking it to the living chain of learning.

This lesson examines two endorsements for the book 'Altarweeh li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih', a commentary on the classical Usul al-Fiqh text 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. Though not containing legal rulings, these taqriz serve as a scholarly seal of approval, connecting the work to the broader tradition of Hanafi learning. Understanding the function of taqriz helps you appreciate how knowledge is transmitted and authenticated in our madhhab.

Guided Path
1
Identify the genre
Recognize that this passage belongs to taqriz (endorsement) literature, a common genre in Islamic scholarly publishing. It is not a legal text but a form of ijazah-like recommendation.
Taqriz often appears at the beginning of a work, authored by respected scholars of the time.
2
Analyze the content of each taqriz
Read each endorsement separately. Note the scholar's name, his credentials, what he praises about the book, and the specific language of approval.
Maulana Yasin Sabir emphasizes research quality; Maulana Shabbir al-Haq Kashmiri confirms proper teaching methodology.
3
Connect to the broader tradition
Understand that taqriz functions as a form of scholarly verification (tawthiq) and connects the reader to the chain of teachers (silsilah).
In Hanafi tradition, such endorsements signal that the work is reliable for study.
4
Evaluate the purpose
Consider why taqriz matters: it builds confidence in the text, especially for students and teachers selecting curriculum materials.
Taqriz also serves a social function, honoring the author and strengthening scholarly networks.

May Allah reward him with the best reward in both worlds. And may Allah have mercy on a servant who says Ameen. Written by the weak servant, Shabbir al-Haq Kashmiri (may Allah forgive him), teacher at Jami'ah Khayr al-Madaris Multan.

Commentary
This passage comprises two endorsements (taqriz) for the book 'Altarweeh li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. The first is by Maulana Muhammad Yasin Sabir, who praises the author Maulana Muhammad Luqman for producing a research-oriented and interesting work. He prays for its acceptance and benefit. The second is by Maulana Shabbir al-Haq Kashmiri, who confirms that the author has properly attended to all teaching aspects of the original text (Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih), making the collection a valuable academic service. Both endorsements highlight the book's utility for students and teachers of Usul al-Fiqh in the Wifaq al-Madaris curriculum. These pages serve as front matter, presenting scholarly validation of the work.

Key Terms
تقریظ (taqriz): A written endorsement or commendation of a book by a respected scholar, often placed at the beginning of a work.
التوضيح والتلويح (Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih): A classical text on Usul al-Fiqh, originally by Sa'd al-Din al-Taftazani (al-Tawdih) and Shams al-Din al-Fanari (al-Talwih).
الترويح (Altarweeh): The name of the commentary being endorsed; literally 'refreshment' or 'solace'.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Understanding Taqriz: Scholarly Endorsements in Hanafi Usul Works
Prefatory scholarly endorsements

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the function of a taqriz in Hanafi usul works and state how it establishes scholarly authority.

Core Idea
A taqriz is a scholarly seal of approval, not mere praise.

When you open a classical Hanafi usul text, you often encounter endorsements from senior scholars. These are not just formalities; they serve specific purposes: verifying the author's competence, attesting to the work's reliability, and connecting it to the teaching tradition. This lesson teaches you to read a taqriz analytically.

Guided Path
1
Identify the endorser's credentials
Note the titles and affiliations given. E.g., 'expert in rational and transmitted sciences', 'teacher of Hadith'. This tells you the weight of the endorsement.
2
Identify the subject and scope
Look for phrases like 'this book relates to the subject of Usul al-Fiqh'. The endorser confirms the work's field and coverage.
3
Recognize pedagogical value statements
Endorsers often comment on clarity, simplicity, and suitability for teaching. E.g., 'extremely simple and easy-to-understand'. This indicates the work's intended audience.
4
Note the connection to curriculum
Mention of 'Dars Nizami' or 'Wifaq al-Madaris curriculum' shows the work fits into an established educational system.
This is key for understanding the work's practical role.

Esteemed Opinion
Expert in rational and transmitted sciences, mujtahid in teaching, full of knowledge and sincerity, our teacher Hadrat Maulana Shabbir al-Ḥaqq Kashmiri (may his shadow be extended), teacher of Hadith and arts at Jami‘a Khayr al-Madaris, Multan.

May Allah reward him with the best reward in both worlds. And may Allah have mercy on whoever says 'Amen.' Written by the weak servant Shabbir al-Ḥaqq Kashmiri, may Allah pardon him, teacher at Jami‘a Khayr al-Madaris, Multan.

Al-Tarwiḥ li-Ḥall al-Tawḍīḥ wa al-Talwīḥ
Esteemed Opinion
Teacher of scholars, comprehensive in rational and transmitted knowledge, Shaykh al-Ḥadith of Jami‘a Makhzan al-‘Ulum Khanpur, Hadrat Maulana Amir Muhammad Ṣāḥib Tunsavi (may his blessings continue), administrator of Jami‘a Faruqiyya Lal Masjid Shergarh, Tehsil Tona, District Dera Ghazi Khan.
Muhammad and his family, and peace be upon his noble messenger. To proceed: 'Al-Tawḍīḥ wa al-Talwīḥ' is a well-known book of Usul al-Fiqh and is part of the Dars Nizami curriculum, which needs no introduction. Various prominent scholars have tested their scholarly strength and written glosses and commentaries on it in different languages, each with their own unique style and manner of writing.
'Rang o bood degar ast / Pasandani aql-e khud / Apna apna har gul' is a famous saying. Where the horsemen of authorship and composition have shown the gems of their ability and scholarly aptitude and stamped their scholarly coin, in this age of scarcity of men, the esteemed, virtuous young teacher of scholars, Hadrat Maulana Muhammad Luqman Ṣāḥib (may his shadow be extended), teacher of Hadith at Dar al-‘Ulum Kabirwala, also took courage on this important subject, undertook the effort of writing, dived into the deep scholarly ocean of the books of predecessors, extracted precious pearls and rare benefits, organized them into words, and presented a great scholarly gift in the form of 'Al-Tarwiḥ li-Ḥall al-Tawḍīḥ wa al-Talwīḥ' for the service of readers and teachers, thereby performing a great service to the science of Usul al-Fiqh. This humble servant has seen various places and numerous pages and folios of this book with a penetrating eye and deep attention, and in all of them, by Allah's will, the author has done justice to the science of Usul al-Fiqh in highly simple, easy-to-understand, and heart-touching words in a research-oriented manner, covering every aspect. May Allah reward him well. The further qualities and features of the book will be observed by respected viewers and readers during study with deep thought and equitable reflection. What need is there for my beautification? 'The beauty of meaning—nature itself adorns the tulip's henna.' Finally, from the bottom of my heart and with utmost humility and submission, I raise my hands in supplication to the Divine court that Allah, by His special grace and generosity, may grant acceptance to this delightful writing of the author, and make it especially beneficial for scholars and students of Usul al-Fiqh.
Source pages p. 34

Commentary
This passage is a preface (front matter) comprising two scholarly endorsements (taqriz) for the book 'Altarweeh Li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih.' The first endorsement is by Maulana Shabbir Haq Kashmiri, a teacher of Hadith at Jamia Khair al-Madaris, Multan. He praises the author, Maulana Muhammad Luqman, for preparing a compilation that explains and clarifies the famous work 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' in Usul al-Fiqh, tailored to the higher curriculum of Wifaq al-Madaris al-Arabiyya, Pakistan. He notes the careful pedagogical attention given and declares it a great scholarly service.

The second endorsement is by Maulana Amir Muhammad Tunsavi, a prominent scholar. He first acknowledges the fame and importance of 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' in the Dars Nizami curriculum, noting that many scholars have written commentaries on it. He then highly commends the author's courage and industry in producing 'Altarweeh,' which extracts pearls from the vast ocean of classical works and presents them in a simple, clear style. The endorsement concludes with a prayer for the book's acceptance and benefit.

This passage functions as front matter, establishing the book's credentials and scholarly value, which is typical for classical Islamic scholarly works. It does not contain any legal rulings or usul principles but rather contextualizes the work for the reader.

Key Terms
تقریظ (taqrīẓ): A scholarly endorsement or commendation written by a respected scholar for a new work, often placed at the beginning of the book to attest to its quality and scholarly value.
اصول فقہ (Uṣūl al-Fiqh): The science of the principles of Islamic jurisprudence; this book is a commentary on a standard text of Hanafi usul.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What is the main function of a taqriz (scholarly endorsement) in a Hanafi usul work?
A) To provide a summary of the book's contents
B) To establish the book's scholarly authority and pedagogical relevance
C) To list all the chapters of the book
D) To criticize previous works on the same subject

Key Takeaway
A taqriz is not mere praise; it is a scholarly validation that helps students and teachers assess a work's reliability and intended use in the Hanafi tradition.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
The Significance of Scholarly Endorsements in the Hanafi Tradition
Front matter endorsements praising the book

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the purpose of a taqriz (scholarly endorsement) in the Hanafi tradition and evaluate how it adds authority to a fiqh/usul text.

Core Idea
A taqriz from a senior scholar authenticates a work's scholarly value and guides students toward reliable sources.

This passage presents two endorsements (taqriz) written by eminent Hanafi scholars for the book 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. Understanding these endorsements helps you recognise how the Hanafi scholarly community vets new works and identifies those worthy of study. Rather than being mere praise, such endorsements serve as scholarly certifications within the tradition.

Guided Path
1
Identify the endorsing scholars and their credentials
Find the names of the two scholars who wrote endorsements and note their positions (e.g., teacher of hadith, head of dar al-ifta). This establishes their authority and relevance.
One is Maulana Amir Muhammad Tonaswi; the other is Mufti Muhammad Abdullah.
2
Determine the subject and structure of the endorsed work
The work is a commentary on al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih. Recognise that this is a foundational text in Hanafi usul al-fiqh within the Dars Nizami curriculum.
The commentary aims to clarify the difficult tashbih and isti'ara (similes and metaphors) in the original.
3
Analyse the specific qualities praised in the endorsements
Look for key phrases: 'easy to understand', 'scholarly manner', 'essence of twenty years of teaching'. These indicate that the commentary is pedagogically effective.
Both endorsements highlight the author's teaching experience and the book's clarity.
4
Understand the role of taqriz in the Hanafi tradition
A taqriz is not merely a recommendation; it signals that the work has been reviewed by established scholars and is considered sound for teaching and learning.
In the Dars Nizami system, such endorsements help students choose reliable commentaries.
5
Evaluate the practical benefit for a student of Hanafi usul
When encountering a new usul text, checking for endorsements from known Hanafi authorities can help you assess its reliability and suitability for your level.
Endorsements do not make a work infallible, but they indicate scholarly confidence.

جامع المعقول والمنقول استاذ العلماء جانشین فقیہ العصر محی السنۃ حضرت مفتی عبد الستار صاحب رحمہ اللہ استاذیم حضرت مولانا مفتی محمد عبد اللہ صاحب رئیس دار الافتاء جامعہ خیر المدارس ملتان
باسمه تعالی محمد و فصلی علی رسولہ الکریم اما بعد
درس نظامی میں چند کتب ایسی ہیں جن کو درس و تدریس میں اعلی مقام حاصل ہے پڑھنے اور پڑھانے والے کو خوب ہمت سے کام لینا پڑتا ہے بلکہ مدرس بنانے میں بشرطیکہ سمجھ کر پڑھے ان کتب کا بنیادی کردار ہے فہم اور فکر میں جلاء اور سر بلندی نصیب ہوتی ہے وہ کتب درج ذیل ہیں بیضاوی شریف ترندی شریف ہدایہ ثالث توضیح تلویح مختصر المعانی شرح جامی وغیرہ پھر ان میں تو ضیح تلویح انتہائی غامض کتاب ہے نفس مسئلہ سمجھنے کے بعد تمثیل و استعارات پر قابو پانا مستقل مرحلہ ہے عزیز محترم حضرت مولانامحمد لقمان صاحب دام مجد ہم مدرس جامعہ دار العلوم کبیر والا خانیوال نے اپنی تمھیس سالہ تدریسی عرق ریزی کا نچوڑ شرح الترویح لحل التوضیح والتلویح کی صورت میں علمی دنیا کے سامنے پیش کیا تعبیرات سادہ لیکن انتہائی پر مغز ہیں ان شاء اللہ طلبائے کرام حضرات مدرسین زید مجدہم کیلئے غوامض تو ضیح کے حل میں یکساں مفید ہوگی دعاء ہے کہ اللہ پاک اسے شرف قبولیت بخشیں اپنی رضائے عالی اور علمی دنیا کیلئے رہنمائی اور ہم سب کی بخشش کا ذریعہ بنائیں اور مؤلف موصوف کیلئے اسے صدقہ جاریہ بنائیں آمین بجاہ وجہہ الکریم و بحق محمد صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم علیک آمین برحمتک یا ارحم الراحمین
بندہ محمد عبد الله عفا عنه الله خادم الافتاء والتدريس بجامعہ خیر المدارس ملتان ۱۴۳۲/۶/۱۴ھ
Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih. Esteemed opinion: Teacher of scholars, master of rational and transmitted sciences, hadith scholar at Jamia Makhzan al-Ulum Khanpur, Hazrat Maulana Amir Muhammad Tonaswi (may his blessings continue), superintendent of Jamia Farooqiya Lal Masjid Sher Garh, Tehsil Tona, District Dera Ghazi Khan. Muhammad and his family be upon his noble messenger. After the thanks: Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih is a famous and well-known book of usul al-fiqh and is included in the Dars Nizami curriculum; it does not need introduction. Various prominent scholars have tested their scholarly strength and written glosses and commentaries in different languages, each with its unique style and mode of writing. 'Each flower has its own fragrance and color, admiration is according to one's own intellect.' It is a famous saying. Where the masters of authorship have shown their ability and scholarly capacity and stamped their scholarly coin, in this age of scarcity of men, the esteemed and excellent young teacher of scholars, Hazrat Maulana Muhammad Luqman (may his shadow be prolonged), teacher of hadith at Darul Uloom Kabirwala, also ventured into this important subject, took up the pen, and diving like a pearl diver into the deep scholarly ocean of the books of the predecessors, extracted precious pearls and rare benefits, and organized them into words, producing 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' as a great scholarly gift for readers and teachers, and performed a great service for the science of usul al-fiqh. I have seen its various places and numerous pages with a deep and thorough examination and all of it. Ma sha Allah, the esteemed author has fulfilled the right of usul al-fiqh in extremely easy and simple-to-understand words in a scholarly manner, covering every aspect. May Allah reward him well. The further merits and features of the book will be observed by the noble viewers and readers at the time of study with deep contemplation and fair and just deliberation. What need is there for my beautification? Nature itself adorns the tulip. Finally, from the bottom of my heart with all humility and submission, raising hands in supplication to the divine court, I pray that Allah Almighty, by His special grace and generosity, grants the author's delightful writing acceptance, and makes it a special help, support, and perfect means for scholars and students of usul al-fiqh for scholarly benefit and advantage, and for the author (may his shadow be prolonged) a cause of complete reward and recompense, and a means of honor and success in religion and world. Ameen, then Ameen. Here we end our speech upon our chosen one, abundant peace. The writer of letters, in need of Allah al-Samad, Amir Muhammad Tonaswi, servant of hadith, Jamia Makhzan al-Ulum wa al-Fuyud, Eidgah Khanpur, District Rahim Yar Khan, 6th Jumada al-Ula 1432 AH, Saturday. Esteemed opinion: Master of rational and transmitted sciences, teacher of scholars, successor of the jurist of the age, reviver of the sunna, Hazrat Mufti Abd al-Sattar (may Allah have mercy on him), our teacher Hazrat Maulana Mufti Muhammad Abdullah, head of Dar al-Ifta at Jamia Khair al-Madaris Multan. In the name of Him, the Exalted. Muhammad and his family be upon his noble messenger. After the thanks: In Dars Nizami, there are several books that hold a high status in teaching and learning; the teacher and student must work hard. Rather, in training a teacher (provided he studies with understanding), these books play a fundamental role; clarity and elevation in understanding and thinking are attained. These books are: Baydawi Sharif, Tirmidhi Sharif, Hidayah Thalith, Tawdih wa Talwih, Mukhtasar al-Ma'ani, Sharh Jami, etc. Among them, Tawdih wa Talwih is an extremely abstruse book; after understanding the issue itself, controlling metaphors and similes is a separate stage. The dear and respected Hazrat Maulana Muhammad Luqman (may his glory last), teacher at Jamia Darul Uloom Kabirwala Khanewal, has presented the essence of his twenty years of teaching effort in the form of the commentary 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' to the scholarly world. The expressions are simple but extremely substantive. Insha Allah, it will be equally beneficial for noble students and respected teachers (may their glory increase) in solving the obscurities of Tawdih. Prayer: May Allah the Pure grant it acceptance, make it a guidance for His high pleasure and the scholarly world, and a means of forgiveness for us all, and make it a continuous charity (sadaqa jariya) for the aforementioned author. Ameen, through the honor of His noble face, and by the right of Muhammad (peace be upon him). Ameen, by Your mercy, O Most Merciful of the merciful. The servant Muhammad Abdullah, may Allah forgive him, servant of ifta and teaching at Jamia Khair al-Madaris Multan, 14 Jumada al-Thani 1432 AH.
Source pages p. 35

Commentary
This passage contains two endorsements (taqriz) written by eminent Hanafi scholars for the book 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' by Maulana Muhammad Luqman. The first endorsement is from Maulana Amir Muhammad Tonaswi, a senior teacher of hadith and rational sciences. He praises the book as a valuable contribution to usul al-fiqh, highlighting that the author has distilled deep insights from classical works into simple language. The second endorsement is from Mufti Muhammad Abdullah, head of Dar al-Ifta at Jamia Khair al-Madaris Multan. He notes that Tawdih wa Talwih is a challenging text within the Dars Nizami curriculum and that this commentary effectively clarifies its difficulties. Both endorsements commend the author's effort and pray for the book's acceptance and benefit to students and teachers. The passage is valuable for understanding the context and reception of this Hanafi usul work.

Key Terms
التوضيح والتلويح (al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih): Two foundational texts in Hanafi usul al-fiqh: al-Tawdih by Sadr al-Shariah and al-Talwih by al-Taftazani, often studied together.
تقریر (taqriz): A formal scholarly endorsement or commendation of a book, typically written by a senior scholar.
درس نظامی (Dars Nizami): The traditional Islamic curriculum used in South Asian madrasas, named after Nizam al-Din Sihalvi.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Key Takeaway
Endorsements by senior Hanafi scholars serve as a guide for students to identify reliable works in usul al-fiqh.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Introduction and Endorsements of Sharh al-Tarwih
Preface and endorsements for a commentary on Tawdih wa Talwih

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain the purpose and significance of a Hanafi usul al-fiqh commentary (sharh) and identify the key features of At-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih as described in its preface.

Core Idea
Sharh clarifies the original; At-Tarwih is a teacher's gift to unlock Tawdih wa Talwih's complexities.

This lesson introduces you to a commentary that serves as a key to one of the most intricate texts in the Hanafi usul al-fiqh curriculum. You will learn about the Dars Nizami tradition, the challenges of studying Tawdih wa Talwih, and how this commentary aims to simplify it for teachers and students. The endorsements highlight the scholarly background of the author and the need for such a work.

Guided Path
1
Identify the type of text
Determine whether this passage is part of the original matn, a commentary, or introductory material. Read the first line and note the presence of endorsements.
This is a preface (muqaddimah) and endorsements (taqariz) for a sharh, not the sharh itself.
2
Recognize the original work
Identify the matn being commented upon: At-Tawdih wa At-Talwih. Understand its place in the Dars Nizami curriculum as a highly advanced text.
At-Tawdih by Sadr al-Sharia and At-Talwih by Taftazani are separate works but studied together.
3
Understand the need for a sharh
From the preface, note why Tawdih wa Talwih is considered difficult: it is intricate (ghamid), involves similes and metaphors (tamthil wa isti'arat), and requires an expert teacher.
The preface states: 'نفس مسئلہ سمجھنے کے بعد تمثیل و استعارات پر قابو پانا مستقل مرحلہ ہے'.
4
Analyze the author's contribution
Examine how Maulana Muhammad Luqman's 25 years of teaching experience distilled into this commentary. The text claims the expressions are simple but highly meaningful.
The commentary is named 'At-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' — 'Tarwih' implies relief from difficulty.
5
Examine the endorsement's perspective
The second endorsement emphasizes the need for expert teachers and verified commentaries. It praises the inclusion of diacritical marks (a'rab), lexical research, and easy style.
The endorsee prays that the work becomes a continuous charity (sadaqa jariya) for the author.

محمد نصلی علی رسولہ الکریم
بسم الله الرحمن الرحیم
اما بعد ! کتب درس نظامی میں توضیح تلویح اصول فقہ کے موضوع پر انتہائی ادق و اغمض کتاب ہے شرح متن کے اجمال و ابہام کو دور کرنے میں معین ہوتی ہے لیکن علامہ تفتازانی شرح کے ساتھ ساتھ جرح و تعدیل سے بھی خوب کام لیتے ہیں متن و جیز شرح ادق کے سمجھانے کیلئے ماہر فن استاذ کی اشد ضرورت ہے اور موجودہ دور میں ماہرین کیلئے بھی شرح محقق کا ہونا ضروری ہے ماشاء اللہ اس سے قبل بھی اردو زبان میں فن تدریس کے آفتاب و ماہتاب علم وفضل کی قد آور شخصیات کی طرف سے توضیح تلویح کی شروعات زیور طبع سے آراستہ پیراستہ ہو کر منظر عام پر آچکی ہیں تاہم لیس العلم عند احد بل العلم عند الجمیع کے تحت دار العلوم عیدگاہ کبیروالا کے مایہ ناز بختی جید استاذ حضرت مولانا محمد لقمان صاحب نے الترویح لحل التوضیح والتلویح کا اضافہ کر کے اہل علم حضرات کی خدمت مین ایک تحقیقی علمی تحفہ پیش کیا ہے جس میں عبارت پر اعراب کلمات کی لغوی تحقیق مرادی مفہوم اور اغراض شارح کو بہت سہل انداز میں پیش کیا ہے دل کی گہرائیوں سے دعا ہے کہ اللہ تعالی برادر موصوف کی اس علمی خدمت کو قبول فرماویں اور مولا نا کیلئے صدقہ جاریہ بنائیں اور اہل علم مدرسین و طلباء کی علمی پیاس بجھائیں آمین ثم آمین
In the name of Him, the Exalted. Muhammad and his family, and peace upon his noble Messenger. As to what follows: In the Dars Nizami curriculum, there are several books that hold a high status in teaching and learning; the teacher and student must exert great effort. Rather, in training a teacher, provided he studies with understanding, these books play a fundamental role. They bring clarity and elevation to intellect and thought. These books are: Baydawi Sharif, Tirmidhi Sharif, Hidayah Thalith, Tawdih wa Talwih, Mukhtasar al-Ma'ani, Sharh Jami, etc. Among these, Tawdih wa Talwih is an extremely intricate book. After understanding the issue itself, mastering the similes and metaphors is a separate stage. Dear respected Maulana Muhammad Luqman (may his glory endure), a teacher at Jamia Darul Uloom Kabirwala, Khanewal, has presented the essence of his twenty-five years of teaching to the scholarly world in the form of 'Sharh al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. The expressions are simple but highly meaningful. By Allah's will, it will be equally beneficial for the dear students and respected teachers (may their glory increase) in solving the intricacies of Tawdih. I pray that Allah the Pure bestows upon it the honor of acceptance, makes it a guide for His pleasure and for the scholarly world, and a means of forgiveness for all of us, and makes it a continuous charity for the aforementioned author. Amin, by the honor of His Noble Face, and by the right of Muhammad, peace be upon him, and his family. Amin, by Your mercy, O Most Merciful of the merciful. At-Tarwih li Hall at-Tawdih wa at-Talwih. Muhammad, we pray upon his noble Messenger. In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful. As to what follows! In the Dars Nizami books, Tawdih wa Talwih on the subject of Usul al-Fiqh is an extremely subtle and intricate book. A commentary helps remove the conciseness and ambiguity of the text, but Allama Taftazani also makes extensive use of criticism and amendment along with the commentary. To understand the concise text and the intricate commentary, an expert teacher is severely needed, and in the present era, even for experts, having a verified commentary is necessary. By Allah's will, before this, explanations of Tawdih wa Talwih in the Urdu language from the sun and moon of the art of teaching, towering personalities of knowledge and virtue, have adorned the pages and come to the public. However, under the principle 'Knowledge is not possessed by one; rather knowledge is by all,' the worthy and brilliant teacher of Darul Uloom Eidgah Kabirwala, Maulana Muhammad Luqman (may his shadow be extended), has added 'At-Tarwih li Hall at-Tawdih wa at-Talwih' and presented a research-based scholarly gift to the people of knowledge. In it, he has presented the diacritical marks, lexical research of words, intended meaning, and the commentator's purposes in a very easy style. From the depths of the heart, I pray that Allah Almighty accepts this scholarly service from the respected brother and makes it a continuous charity for Maulana, and quenches the scholarly thirst of scholars, teachers, and students. Amin, then Amin.
Source pages p. 36

Commentary
This passage is the preface and endorsements (taqariz) for the book 'At-Tarwih li Hall at-Tawdih wa at-Talwih', a commentary on the classical Hanafi usul al-fiqh text 'At-Tawdih wa at-Talwih' by Sadr al-Sharia and Taftazani. The text begins in Urdu with an introduction by a scholar, praising the Dars Nizami curriculum and the difficulty of the book being commented upon. It introduces the author, Maulana Muhammad Luqman, and his work, describing it as a simple yet profound explanation. The second part contains an endorsement by another scholar, emphasizing the intricate nature of the original and the need for expert teachers, and praising the new commentary for its clarity and research. The commentary itself is not yet into the technical fiqh; it is purely introductory.

Key Terms
التَّوْضِيحُ وَالتَّلْوِيحُ (at-Tawdih wa at-Talwih): The base text (matn) by Sadr al-Sharia (al-Tawdih) and its supercommentary (al-Talwih) by Sa'd al-Din al-Taftazani, a foundational work in Hanafi usul al-fiqh.
شرح (sharh): A commentary that explains the original text, here referring to the book being introduced.

Key Terms from Source Passage

C) To criticize the classical authors Sadr al-Sharia and Taftazani.
D) To translate At-Tawdih wa at-Talwih into Arabic.

Key Takeaway
At-Tarwih is a teacher's commentary designed to unlock the complexities of the Hanafi usul al-fiqh classic At-Tawdih wa At-Talwih.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
The Role of Scholarly Endorsements (Taqrizat) in Hanafi Scholarship
Two taqrizat praising the commentary and its authors

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain the purpose of taqrizat and identify the chain of scholarly authority referenced in endorsements.

Core Idea
Taqrizat connect a new commentary to the authoritative tradition, validating its reliability.

Scholarly endorsements, or taqrizat, are a time-honored tradition in Islamic learning. They serve to establish the credibility of a new work by linking it to recognized authorities and expressing the confidence of established scholars. In this lesson, we examine two such endorsements for the commentary 'Al-Tarwih' on the foundational Usul al-Fiqh texts 'Al-Tawdih' and 'Al-Talwih', which themselves are pillars of the Hanafi curriculum.

Guided Path
1
Identify the authors of the endorsements
Read the names and titles of the endorsers. Note their positions and institutional affiliations. This establishes the weight of the endorsements.
Both are respected scholars in Dar al-Ulum and Jami'a Khair al-Madaris.
2
Analyze the description of the original texts
The endorsements discuss the original works 'Al-Tawdih' by Sadr al-Shariah and 'Al-Talwih' by Taftazani. Understand their place in Hanafi Usul al-Fiqh and why they are considered subtle and difficult.
These texts form the basis of the commentary.
3
Examine the commentary's features
The endorsements list the commentary's contents: diacritics, translation, lexical investigations, rhetorical clarifications, etc. This shows the comprehensive nature of the work.
The word 'Al-Tarwih' means 'refreshment' – alluding to making the difficult easy.
4
Understand the function of the endorsements
Reflect on why the endorsements are included: to validate the commentary's quality, to attract readers, and to place it within the continuum of Hanafi scholarship.
This is a common feature in traditional Islamic academic publishing.

اما بعد ! اصول فقہ علوم عالیہ میں سے اہم ترین علم ہے جس سے فقہ وفقاہت کے اصول وقواعد اور حقائق کا ادراک حاصل ہوتا ہے علماءمحققین نے ہر دور میں اس علم کے بارہ میں محنت کی علامہ صدر الشریعہ الاصغر عبید اللہ بن مسعود المتوفی ۵۷۴۷ اور علامہ سعد الدین مسعود بن عمر تفتازانی المتوفی ۷۹۲ ھ ہر دونوں جبال علم میں سے ہیں اول الذکر کی توضیح اور ثانی کی شرح تلویح علم اصول فقہ کی معیاری بنیادی کتابیں ہیں
ہر دور میں یہ شامل نصاب تعلیم رہیں نیز فن اصول فقہ میں یہ فوائد اور مقاصد کے اعتبار سے انتہائی اہمیت و عظمت کی حامل ہیں لیکن اس کے ساتھ ساتھ انتہائی دقیق بھی ہیں ہر کس و ناکس کیلئے ان سے استفادہ دشوار تھا اور طلباء علوم عربیہ اس کو سمجھنے میں کافی وقت محسوس کرتے تھے اس لئے ان کی اہمیت و عظمت کے پیش نظر اس بات کی ضرورت تھی کہ اس کی کوئی مفصل اردو شرح مرتب کی جائے محترم حضرت مولانا محمد لقمان صاحب استاذ الحدیث دار العلوم کبیر والا کواللہ نے توفیق دی اور انہوں نے اس کی عبارت اعراب ترجمہ سمیت ایک بہترین شرح لکھی ہے
یہ شرح کیا ہے فوائد نکات تحقیقات و تدقیقات مهمه مسائل شارده و وارده اشارات رموز و اسرار مطويات مکنونات و مخفیات کا حسین مرصع و خوبصورت گلدستہ اور نیچے موتیوں کی چمکدار مالا ہے علماء وطلباء کیلئے نعمت عظمی ہے حق جل شانہ سے دعا ہے کہ جلد از جلد اس کا بقیہ حصہ بھی طبع کرانے کی توفیق عطا فرمائے اور اس کو حضرت مولانامحمد لقمان صاحب و جملہ معاونین کے رفع درجات کا سبب بنائے

الترويح لحَلَّ التَّوْضِيحِ وَالتَّنْويج

پیر طریقت رہبر شریعت زاہد عن الدنیا عارف باللہ استاذیم حضرت مولانا محمد عابد صاحب مدنی مدظله العالی استاذ التفسير والحدیث جامعہ خیر المدارس ملتان
بسم الله الرحمن الرحیم
قال النبی صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم من يرد اللہ بہ خیر اینفقہ فی الدین اسلام ایک ابدی دین ہے قیامت تک کے انسانوں کیلئے رہبر و رہنما ہے قرن اول سے قیامت تک امت محمدیہ میں ایک جماعت ایسی رہے گی جو دین کا صحیح فہم رکھنے والی ہوگی اور انسانیت کو صراط مستقیم کی دعوت دے گی کتاب وسنت کے فہم کو ہم فقہ کہ سکتے ہیں اسی ذیل میں اصول فقہ ایک جلیل القدر عظیم فن ہے جو صد ر اول سے علماء امت کا مخدوم رہا ہے
اسی فن کی ایک مہتم بالشان کتاب التوضیح والتلویح ہے جو ہماری نصابی کتاب ہے عزیز مولوی محمد لقمان سلمہ الرحمن نے بڑی جانفشانی سے اس کی اردو شرح تحریر کی ہے جو الترویح لحل التوضیح والتلویح کے نام سے موسوم ہے جو کہ اعراب ترجمہ تحقیقات لغویہ ومراد یہ اغراض شارح فوائد نافعہ وافیہ پر مشتمل ہے نیز اس میں صنعات بلاغت استعارات و تمثیلات و غیر ہاکی وضاحت احسن انداز میں کی گئی ہے دعا ہے کہ اللہ کریم عزیز موصوف کو علماء راشین کے فیضان سے حظ وافر عطاء فرمائے اور کتاب کو اہل علم کیلئے مفید بنائے آمین

یکے از خدام حضرت بہلوی ۱۳؍ جمادی الاولی ۱۴۳۱۲ھ
Al-Tarwih li-Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih. Noble opinion: Expert in rational and transmitted sciences, embodiment of sincerity, teacher of scholars, our master Mawlana Abd al-Sattar, deputy head of hadith at Dar al-Ulum Eidgah Kabirwala. In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful. To proceed: Usul al-Fiqh is among the most important of the lofty sciences, through which the principles, rules, and realities of fiqh and juristic understanding are attained. The verifying scholars in every era have labored over this science. Allamah Sadr al-Shariah al-Asghar Ubayd Allah ibn Mas'ud (d. 747 AH) and Allamah Sa'd al-Din Mas'ud ibn 'Umar al-Taftazani (d. 792 AH) are both mountains of knowledge. The former's al-Tawdih and the latter's al-Talwih are standard foundational books in Usul al-Fiqh. In every era, these have been included in the curriculum, and in the field of Usul al-Fiqh, they are of utmost importance and grandeur in terms of benefits and objectives. But at the same time, they are extremely subtle; it was difficult for every Tom, Dick, and Harry to benefit from them, and students of Arabic sciences found them time-consuming to understand. Therefore, considering their importance and grandeur, there was a need to prepare a detailed Urdu commentary. The respected Mawlana Muhammad Luqman, teacher of hadith at Dar al-Ulum Kabirwala, was given success by Allah, and he wrote an excellent commentary including the text with diacritics and translation. What is this commentary? It is a beautiful, decorated bouquet and a shining necklace of pearls beneath: benefits, points, investigations, verifications, important issues, rare and common [issues], indications, symbols, secrets, contents, hidden things, and concealed matters. It is a great blessing for scholars and students. Prayer to the Lord of Majesty that soon He grant success to publish its remaining part and make it a cause for the elevation of ranks of Mawlana Muhammad Luqman and all assistants. This is a prayer from me and everyone. Amen. Abd al-Sattar, teacher at Dar al-Ulum Kabirwala.

Al-Tarwih li-Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih. Noble opinion: The spiritual master, guide of Shariah, ascetic of the world, knower of Allah, our teacher Mawlana Muhammad Abid Madani, may his shadow be extended, teacher of Tafsir and Hadith at Jami'a Khair al-Madaris Multan. In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful. The Prophet (peace be upon him) said: 'Whoever Allah desires good for, He gives him understanding of the religion (fiqh).' Islam is an eternal religion, a guide for mankind until the Day of Judgment. From the first century until Judgment Day, there will be a group in the Ummah of Muhammad that possesses correct understanding of the religion and invites humanity to the straight path. We can call the understanding of the Book and Sunnah 'fiqh'. In this context, Usul al-Fiqh is a great and magnificent art that has been served by the scholars of the Ummah since the first century. A highly important book in this art is al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih, which is our textbook. The dear Mawlana Muhammad Luqman (may Allah preserve him) has with great effort written an Urdu commentary on it, named Al-Tarwih li-Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih, which includes: diacritics, translation, lexical investigations, intended meanings, the commentator's goals, and beneficial sufficient points. Also, it clarifies in a beautiful style the figures of rhetoric, metaphors, similes, etc. Prayer that Allah Almighty grant the dear mentioned person abundant share from the effusion of the rightly guided scholars and make the book beneficial for the people of knowledge. Amen. And our last call is that all praise is due to Allah, Lord of the worlds. Muhammad Abid, may he be pardoned, teacher at Jami'a Khair al-Madaris Multan. One of the servants of Hadrat Bahlwi. 13 Jamadi al-Awwal 1431 AH.
Source pages p. 38

Commentary
This passage contains two endorsements (taqrizat) for the commentary 'Al-Tarwih li-Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. The first endorsement, by Mawlana Abd al-Sattar, highlights the importance of Usul al-Fiqh and introduces the original works 'Al-Tawdih' by Sadr al-Shariah and 'Al-Talwih' by Taftazani. He praises the commentary by Mawlana Muhammad Luqman as a detailed Urdu explanation that clarifies the difficult points of these texts. The second endorsement, by Mawlana Muhammad Abid Madani, similarly extols the value of Usul al-Fiqh and the commentary, noting that it includes linguistic research, rhetorical clarifications, and other beneficial content. Both endorsers pray for the success and acceptance of the work. This front matter establishes the book's credibility and purpose within the Hanafi tradition of Usul al-Fiqh.

Key Terms
تقرظ (taqriz): A formal scholarly endorsement, usually written by a respected scholar to validate a new work.
صدر الشریعة الاصغر (Sadr al-Shariah al-Asghar): Title of Ubayd Allah ibn Mas'ud, a Hanafi jurist and author of 'Al-Tawdih', a standard Usul al-Fiqh text.
تلویح (Al-Talwih): A commentary by Sa'd al-Din al-Taftazani on 'Al-Tawdih', forming a core text in Hanafi Usul al-Fiqh.
ترویح (Al-Tarwih): The title of the commentary being endorsed, meaning 'refreshment' or 'ease'.

Key Terms from Source Passage

According to the passage, who authored the original works 'Al-Tawdih' and 'Al-Talwih'?
A) Al-Tawdih by Sadr al-Shariah, Al-Talwih by Taftazani
B) Al-Tawdih by Taftazani, Al-Talwih by Sadr al-Shariah
C) Both by Sadr al-Shariah
D) Both by Taftazani

Key Takeaway
Endorsements (taqrizat) serve as a scholarly chain of authentication, linking a new commentary to the established tradition and assuring readers of its quality and reliability.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
5 min
Understanding Scholarly Endorsements and the Textual Tradition in Hanafi Usul al-Fiqh
Two scholarly endorsements for an Urdu commentary on Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the role of taqrizat (scholarly endorsements) in the Hanafi textual tradition and locate the commentary Al-Tarwih within the lineage of Usul al-Fiqh texts.

Core Idea
Endorsements (taqrizat) authenticate a text within the scholarly chain, linking it to the living tradition.

This passage presents two taqrizat (scholarly endorsements) for the book 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih', an Urdu commentary on the classical Hanafi usul text 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. Understanding such endorsements helps you appreciate how texts are vetted and passed down in the Islamic scholarly tradition. By analyzing these endorsements, you will learn to identify the key elements of a taqriz and its function in the curriculum.

Guided Path
1
Identify the celebrated text
First, note the book being endorsed: 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. Recognize that it is a commentary (sharh) on the foundational usul work 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'.
The base text 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' is itself a commentary on 'Tanqih al-Usul' by Sadr al-Shariah.
2
Identify the endorsing scholars
Note the two scholars: Maulana Muhammad 'Abid Madani (teacher at Jamia Khair al-Madaris, Multan) and Mufti Muhammad Hasan (of Jamia Madania Jadid, Lahore). Their positions give weight to the endorsement.
Both are respected Hanafi scholars, which strengthens the commentary's credibility in the tradition.
3
Analyze the purpose of the endorsements
The endorsements highlight the importance of understanding religion, the role of Usul al-Fiqh, and the effort of the commentator. They serve to commend the work to students and affirm its value.
Taqrizat typically include supplications (dua) for the author and readers.
4
Observe the rhetorical structure
Note the opening hadith (Man yuridillahu bihi khairan…), references to Quranic verses (Inna nahnu nazzalna al-dhikr…), and the concluding prayers. This is a standard format for scholarly endorsements.
The structure mirrors that of a short academic preface.

بسم الله الرحمن الرحیم
قال النبی صلی اللہ علیہ وسلم من يرد اللہ بہ خیر اینفقہ فی الدین اسلام ایک ابدی دین ہے قیامت تک کے انسانوں کیلئے رہبر و رہنما ہے قرن اول سے قیامت تک امت محمدیہ میں ایک جماعت ایسی رہے گی جو دین کا صحیح فہم رکھنے والی ہوگی اور انسانیت کو صراط مستقیم کی دعوت دے گی کتاب وسنت کے فہم کو ہم فقہ کہ سکتے ہیں اسی ذیل میں اصول فقہ ایک جلیل القدر عظیم فن ہے جو صد ر اول سے علماء امت کا مخدوم رہا ہے
اسی فن کی ایک مہتم بالشان کتاب التوضیح والتلویح ہے جو ہماری نصابی کتاب ہے عزیز مولوی محمد لقمان سلمہ الرحمن نے بڑی جانفشانی سے اس کی اردو شرح تحریر کی ہے جو الترویح لحل التوضیح والتلویح کے نام سے موسوم ہے جو کہ اعراب ترجمہ تحقیقات لغویہ ومراد یہ اغراض شارح فوائد نافعہ وافیہ پر مشتمل ہے نیز اس میں صنعات بلاغت استعارات و تمثیلات و غیر ہاکی وضاحت احسن انداز میں کی گئی ہے دعا ہے کہ اللہ کریم عزیز موصوف کو علماء راشین کے فیضان سے حظ وافر عطاء فرمائے اور کتاب کو اہل علم کیلئے مفید بنائے آمین
و آخر دعوانا ان الحمد لله رب العلمین
محمد عابد عفی عنہ مدرس جامعہ خیر المدارس ملتان

محمد حسن عفی عنہ
Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih. Noble opinion. The spiritual guide, ascetic in the world, knower of Allah, our teacher Hadhrat Maulana Muhammad 'Abid Madani (may his shadow be extended), teacher of Tafsir and Hadith at Jamia Khair al-Madaris, Multan. In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful. The Prophet (peace be upon him) said: 'Whoever Allah desires good for, He gives him understanding of the religion.' Islam is an eternal religion, a guide and leader for mankind until the Day of Judgment. From the first century until the Day of Judgment, there will remain a group in the Ummah of Muhammad that possesses correct understanding of the religion and will invite humanity to the straight path. We can call the understanding of the Book and the Sunnah 'Fiqh'. In this context, Usul al-Fiqh is a great and magnificent discipline that has been served by the scholars of the Ummah since the first century. Among the highly regarded books of this discipline is Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih, which is our textbook. Dear Maulvi Muhammad Luqman (may Allah have mercy on him) has written an Urdu commentary on it with great effort, named 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. This commentary includes diacritical marks, translation, lexical investigations, meanings, objectives of the commentator, beneficial and comprehensive benefits, and it also contains rhetorical devices, metaphors, analogies, etc., clarified in an excellent manner. Prayer: May Allah grant the aforementioned dear person abundant share from the blessings of the rightly-guided scholars, and make this book beneficial for the people of knowledge. Amen. And our final call is that all praise is due to Allah, the Lord of the worlds. Muhammad 'Abid (forgiven) teacher at Jamia Khair al-Madaris, Multan. One of the servants of Hadhrat Bahlawi, 13 Jumada al-Awwal 14312 AH. Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih. Noble opinion. Possessor of principles and branches, beloved of scholars and students, the master of teaching Hadhrat Maulana Mufti Muhammad Hasan (may his blessings continue) of Jamia Madania Jadid, Lahore. In His name, exalted. May blessings be upon His noble Messenger. After that: The great blessing and grace of Allah, the Lord of Majesty, is that He Himself has taken the responsibility of protecting His clear religion, as the divine command says: 'Indeed, We have sent down the Reminder, and indeed We are its guardians.' In the world of means, He arranged for its protection by choosing a group of the people of truth for guarding all branches of His clear religion, who will continue to perform the duty of protecting and safeguarding all branches of the clear religion until the Day of Judgment. Among the fortunate personalities of the caravan of truth is a noble personality, our great teacher of the religious, academic, and spiritual center Darul Uloom Kabirwala, Maulana Muhammad Luqman (may his blessings continue), who has written an excellent commentary on the very detailed book of Usul al-Fiqh taught in religious schools, Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih, named 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. Its study will, God willing, prove beneficial for readers. I humbly request in the court of Allah that He accept this noble effort and make it a means of attaining His pleasure and approval. Amen. In need of prayers, Muhammad Hasan (forgiven).
Source pages p. 39

Commentary
This passage contains two scholarly endorsements (taqrizat) for the book 'Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih', a commentary on the classical Hanafi usul text 'Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. The first endorsement is by Maulana Muhammad 'Abid Madani, a teacher at Jamia Khair al-Madaris, Multan. He emphasizes the importance of understanding the religion, and presents the commentary as a valuable aid for students of usul al-fiqh. The second endorsement is by Mufti Muhammad Hasan from Jamia Madania Jadid, Lahore. He highlights the significance of protecting the religion and praises the effort of the author, Maulana Muhammad Luqman, in producing this commentary. Both scholars pray for the acceptance and benefit of the work.

Key Terms
التوضیح والتلویح (Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih): A foundational textbook in Hanafi Usul al-Fiqh, written by Sadr al-Shariah and commented upon by Taftazani.
الترویح لحل التوضیح والتلویح (Al-Tarwih li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih): An Urdu commentary on Al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih written by Maulana Muhammad Luqman.

Key Terms from Source Passage

B) A standalone book on Usul al-Fiqh

D) A collection of hadith

Key Takeaway
Scholarly endorsements (taqrizat) situate a text within the broader tradition, attesting to its value and authenticity.

Introduction and Front Matter
beginner
6 min
Understanding Taqriz: Scholarly Endorsements in Hanafi Usul
Two scholarly endorsements for a Hanafi usul commentary

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain the purpose of a taqriz in Islamic scholarly tradition and identify the author, commentator, and original text of 'Altarweeh li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'.

Core Idea
Taqriz establish scholarly authority and recommend the commentary as a reliable guide to Taftazani's usul.

Before diving into the content of a scholarly commentary, it is essential to understand the endorsements (taqriz) that preface it. These are not mere formalities; they serve as scholarly certifications, affirming the work's accuracy, usefulness, and adherence to the school. In this lesson, you will analyze two such taqriz for the Hanafi usul commentary 'Altarweeh' and learn how to extract key information about the text's lineage and authority.

Guided Path
1
Identify the Taqriz Authors
Locate the names of the scholars who wrote the endorsements. They are Maulana Mufti Muhammad Hasan (first taqriz) and Maulana Muhammad Ismail Arshad (second taqriz). Note their titles (e.g., 'investigator of the age', 'teacher of scholars') which indicate their scholarly standing.
Their status lends weight to the recommendation.
2
Identify the Endorsed Work
Find the title of the commentary being praised: 'Altarweeh li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. Also note the original base text it explains: 'al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' by Allama Taftazani.
The word 'Hall' in the title means 'solving' or 'unlocking' difficulties.
3
Analyze the Praise
Examine the qualities highlighted: the author's effort, the commentary's precision, completeness, and sufficiency for understanding the base text. For example, the second taqriz says 'with no further addition needed'.
Such language emphasizes that this commentary is comprehensive.
4
Connect to the Hanafi Usul Tradition
Understand that 'al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih' is a renowned but dense Hanafi usul work. Commentaries like 'Altarweeh' serve to make it accessible, aiding students and scholars in deriving rulings (istinbat).
The endorsements confirm the commentary's role in preserving and transmitting the school's methodology.

Altarweeh li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih

Noble Endorsement
Embodying the principles and branches, beloved of scholars and students, chief teacher, Hazrat Maulana Mufti Muhammad Hasan (may his blessings endure), Jamia Madania Jadeed, Lahore.
In the name of Allah. Praise and salutations upon His noble Messenger.
After praise! A great favor and grace of Allah, Lord of Majesty, that He Himself has taken the responsibility of protecting His clear religion, as His divine command says: 'Indeed We have sent down the Remembrance and indeed We are its guardians.' And in the world of means, He arranged its protection thus: Allah chose a group of people of truth to guard all departments of His clear religion, who will continue to perform the duty of protecting and guarding all departments of the clear religion until the Day of Judgment. Among the fortunate personalities of the caravan of truth is a noble personality: our great spiritual and academic center Darul Uloom Kabirwala's great teacher, Maulana Muhammad Luqman (may his blessings endure), who with great effort wrote a very fine commentary on the extremely precise book of usul al-fiqh taught in religious schools, Tawdih wa Talwih, named 'Altarweeh li Hall al-Tawdih wa al-Talwih'. Its study will, Allah willing, prove beneficial for readers. In the court of Allah is the request that He accept this noble effort in His court and make it a means of attaining His pleasure and approval. Amen.
In need of supplication
Muhammad Hasan (forgiven)
